[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m96[0m[39m:        link_depends: libdav1d_af,[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m97[0m[39m:        build_by_default: false,[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m98[0m[39m:        dependencies : [0m[1;39m[[0m[39mthread_dependency[0m[1;39m][0m[39m,[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m99[0m[39m:        kwargs: fuzzer_link_lang[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m100[0m[39m:        [0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<code>[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtests/libfuzzer/meson.buil[0m[1;92md:61[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m66[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;92m61:da[0m[39mv1d_fuzzer_mt = [0m[1;35mexecutable[0m[1;39m([0m[32m'dav1d_fuzzer_mt'[0m[39m,[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m62[0m[39m:    dav1d_fuzzer_sources,[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m63[0m[39m:    include_directories: dav1d_inc_dirs,[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m64[0m[39m:    c_args: [0m[1;39m[[0m[32m'-DDAV1D_MT_FUZZING'[0m[1;39m][0m[39m,[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m65[0m[39m:    link_args: fuzzer_ldflags,[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m66[0m[39m:    link_with : libdav1d,[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<code>[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexamples/meson.buil[0m[1;92md:66[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m74[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m66[0m[39m:        rev_target,[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m67[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m68[0m[39m:        link_with : [0m[1;39m[[0m[39mlibdav1d, dav1d_input_objs[0m[1;39m][0m[39m,[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m69[0m[39m:        include_directories : [0m[1;39m[[0m[39mdav1d_inc_dirs[0m[1;39m][0m[39m,[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m70[0m[39m:        dependencies : [0m[1;39m[[0m[39mgetopt_dependency, dav1dplay_deps[0m[1;39m][0m[39m,[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m71[0m[39m:        install : true,[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m72[0m[39m:        c_args : dav1dplay_cflags,[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m73[0m[39m:    [0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;92m74:e[0m[39mndif[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<code>[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtests/libfuzzer/meson.buil[0m[1;92md:61[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m70[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;92m61:da[0m[39mv1d_fuzzer_mt = [0m[1;35mexecutable[0m[1;39m([0m[32m'dav1d_fuzzer_mt'[0m[39m,[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m62[0m[39m:    dav1d_fuzzer_sources,[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m63[0m[39m:    include_directories: dav1d_inc_dirs,[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m64[0m[39m:    c_args: [0m[1;39m[[0m[32m'-DDAV1D_MT_FUZZING'[0m[1;39m][0m[39m,[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m65[0m[39m:    link_args: fuzzer_ldflags,[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m66[0m[39m:    link_with : libdav1d,[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m67[0m[39m:    build_by_default: true,[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m68[0m[39m:    dependencies : [0m[1;39m[[0m[39mthread_dependency[0m[1;39m][0m[39m,[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m69[0m[39m:    kwargs: fuzzer_link_lang[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m70[0m[39m:    [0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Root Cause Analysis[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The fuzzer binaries [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`dav1d_fuzzer_mt` and its siblings[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m are declared via [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mMesonâ€™s `[0m[1;35mexecutable[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` in `tests/libfuzzer/meson.build` but lack any `install:` [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdirective.  [0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - OSS-Fuzzâ€™s build pipeline relies on a `ninja install` into a custom `prefix` [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39mmounted as `[0m[35m/[0m[95mout[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m so that `[0m[35m/out/[0m[39m<fuzzer_name>` exists and is marked executable.  [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Without `install: true`, Meson does not include these fuzzer executables in [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe install tree, or installs them with default data-file permissions [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m644[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mleading to â€œPermission deniedâ€ [0m[1;39m([0m[39mexit code [0m[1;36m126[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m when the runner tries to execute [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[35m/out/[0m[95mdav1d_fuzzer_mt[0m[39m`.[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Patch Location[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - File: `tests/libfuzzer/meson.build`[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Sections defining `dav1d_fuzzer` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline ~[0m[1;36m51[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and `dav1d_fuzzer_mt` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline ~[0m[1;36m61[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mand any other fuzz-related executables [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., `dav1d_fuzzer_mem`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Proposed Changes[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   A. Add Meson install directives to each fuzzer target:[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```meson[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      dav1d_fuzzer_mt = [0m[1;35mexecutable[0m[1;39m([0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[32m'dav1d_fuzzer_mt'[0m[39m,[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        dav1d_fuzzer_sources,[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        include_directories: dav1d_inc_dirs,[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        c_args: [0m[1;39m[[0m[32m'-DDAV1D_MT_FUZZING'[0m[1;39m][0m[39m,[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        link_args: fuzzer_ldflags,[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        link_with: libdav1d,[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        build_by_default: true,[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        dependencies: [0m[1;39m[[0m[39mthread_dependency[0m[1;39m][0m[39m,[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        kwargs: fuzzer_link_lang,[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        install: true,[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        install_dir: [0m[1;35mget_option[0m[1;39m([0m[32m'prefix'[0m[1;39m)[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - `install: true` ensures Mesonâ€™s `ninja install` step copies the binary into[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe install prefix.  [0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - `install_dir: [0m[1;35mget_option[0m[1;39m([0m[32m'prefix'[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` places the binary directly under the [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mprefix directory [0m[1;39m([0m[39mOSS-Fuzz mounts this as `[0m[35m/[0m[95mout[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, matching `run_fuzzer`â€™s [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minvocation of `[0m[35m/out/[0m[95mdav1d_fuzzer_mt[0m[39m`.[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   B. Mirror the same install flags for other fuzzers [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`dav1d_fuzzer`, [0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`dav1d_fuzzer_mem`, etc.[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m to maintain consistency when building with [0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`-[0m[33mDfuzzing_engine[0m[39m=[0m[35mlibfuzzer[0m[39m`.[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Implementation Steps[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   a. Open `tests/libfuzzer/meson.build`.  [0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   b. Locate the `[0m[1;35mexecutable[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` calls for each fuzzer target.  [0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   c. Append the two parameters:  [0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - `install: true`  [0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - `install_dir: [0m[1;35mget_option[0m[1;39m([0m[32m'prefix'[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`  [0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   d. Save and commit the change.  [0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   e. Re-run the OSS-Fuzz build [0m[1;39m([0m[39mwhich invokes `meson [0m[33m...[0m[39m [0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m-[0m[33mDprefix[0m[39m=$PWD/build/out/dav1d` then `ninja && ninja install`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   f. Verify inside the Docker runner that `[0m[35m/out/[0m[95mdav1d_fuzzer_mt[0m[39m` exists and is [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexecutable:[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      docker run --rm -v [0m[35m/[0m[39mâ€¦[0m[35m/build/out/[0m[95mdav1d[0m[39m:[0m[35m/[0m[95mout[0m[39m [0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mghcr.io/aixcc-finals/base-runner:v1.[0m[1;36m3.0[0m[39m ls -l [0m[35m/out/[0m[95mdav1d_fuzzer_mt[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      # Expected: -rwxr-xr-x[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Justification[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Mesonâ€™s `install:` mechanism is the canonical way to include build artifacts [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39min the install tree with proper modes.  [0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This approach does not alter any external dependencies, harness code, or test [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcode. It only augments the existing fuzzer declarations.  [0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - It preserves all `build_by_default`, compiler arguments, linking flags, and [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmulti-threading logic.  [0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The fix aligns the fuzzer targets with the example CLI tools [0m[1;39m([0m[39mwhich already [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39muse `install: true`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and ensures seamless execution under the OSS-Fuzz runner.[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. Potential Side Effects & Mitigation[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Local installs [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`ninja install` to system prefix[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m will also install fuzzers [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39munder the prefix root. If this is undesirable for end-users, one could guard the [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minstall directive under:[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     if fuzzing_engine != [0m[32m'none'[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       install: true,[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       install_dir: [0m[1;35mget_option[0m[1;39m([0m[32m'prefix'[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m,[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     endif[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     so that only fuzz-engine builds install the fuzzers.  [0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No impact on existing Meson-based tests, library packaging, or non-fuzzer [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mworkflows.[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m7[0m[39m. Verification[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - After patch, reproduce the OSS-Fuzz runner failure; the fuzzer should now [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexecute, proceed past the permission error, and begin fuzzing as expected.[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mCode Range for Patch:[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<code_range>tests/libfuzzer/meson.buil[0m[1;92md:61[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m70[0m[39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_range[0m[39m>[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<code>[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtests/libfuzzer/meson.buil[0m[1;92md:61[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m70[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;92m61:da[0m[39mv1d_fuzzer_mt = [0m[1;35mexecutable[0m[1;39m([0m[32m'dav1d_fuzzer_mt'[0m[39m,[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m62[0m[39m:    dav1d_fuzzer_sources,[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m63[0m[39m:    include_directories: dav1d_inc_dirs,[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m64[0m[39m:    c_args: [0m[1;39m[[0m[32m'-DDAV1D_MT_FUZZING'[0m[1;39m][0m[39m,[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m65[0m[39m:    link_args: fuzzer_ldflags,[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m66[0m[39m:    link_with : libdav1d,[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m67[0m[39m:    build_by_default: true,[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m68[0m[39m:    dependencies : [0m[1;39m[[0m[39mthread_dependency[0m[1;39m][0m[39m,[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m69[0m[39m:    kwargs: fuzzer_link_lang[0m                                                     [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Root Cause Analysis  [0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The Meson build definitions for both `dav1d_fuzzer` and `dav1d_fuzzer_mt` [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdeclare `build_by_default: true` but omit the `install: true` attribute.  [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Without `install: true`, `ninja install` does _not_ place these executables [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minto the install prefix. OSS-Fuzzâ€™s build wrapper then has nothing to copy into [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`$OUT`, or copies stub files without the execute bit, leading to a non-executable [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbinary at `[0m[35m/out/[0m[95mdav1d_fuzzer_mt[0m[39m` and the â€œPermission deniedâ€ error.[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Strategic Patch  [0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   A. In `tests/libfuzzer/meson.build`, for both fuzzer targets:  [0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Add the Meson keyword `install: true` so that `ninja install` will install [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe executables into the prefix with proper permissions.  [0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Place `install: true` alongside the existing `build_by_default: true` line [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfor clarity.[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   B. No changes to harness or fuzzing logic. Harness scripts will pick up the [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnow-executable binary under `$OUT` without modification.  [0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   C. No changes to test code or external dependencies.[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Implementation Steps  [0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. Open `tests/libfuzzer/meson.build`.  [0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. Locate the block for `dav1d_fuzzer` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines ~[0m[1;36m51[0m[39mâ€“[0m[1;36m60[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m. Amend as follows:[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Before the closing parenthesis, insert:[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        ```[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        build_by_default: true,[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        install: true,[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        ```[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m. Locate the block for `dav1d_fuzzer_mt` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines ~[0m[1;36m61[0m[39mâ€“[0m[1;36m70[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m. Amend similarly:[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        ```[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        build_by_default: true,[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        install: true,[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        ```[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m. Re-run the OSS-Fuzz build:[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ninja -C outbuild[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ninja -C outbuild install[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      Verify the binaries appear in the install prefix [0m[1;39m([0m[39mand thus in `[0m[35m/[0m[95mout[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m with [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexecute permissions [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`-rwxr-xr-x`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Justification  [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Adding `install: true` is the standard Meson mechanism to ensure executables [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mare included in the installation step with correct file modes.  [0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This change is minimal, scoped only to the two fuzzer targets, preserving all [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexisting logic and build dependencies.  [0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - It aligns with other projectsâ€™ Meson fuzz targets, which similarly require [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`install: true` for OSS-Fuzz integration.  [0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No side effects on normal library or application builds, as the fuzzer targets[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mare only used under the fuzzing build path.  [0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Validation  [0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - After applying the patch, `ls -l outbuild/install/bin/dav1d_fuzzer_mt` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mor [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mequivalent prefix[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m must show the execute bit.  [0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Running the fuzzer with the harness [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`run_fuzzer dav1d_fuzzer_mt â€¦`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m should [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mproceed past the launch step without â€œPermission denied.â€  [0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Existing regression and unit tests remain unaffected.[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtests/libfuzzer/dav1d_fuzzer_mt@NO_OOM:[0m[1;36m13[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m24[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m13[0m[39m:[0m[33mthis_dir[0m[39m=$[0m[1;39m([0m[39mdirname [0m[32m"$0"[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                         [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m15[0m[39m:# chmod the actual binary so that it's not picked up by our infrastructure[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m16[0m[39m:# until it's actually ready[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;92m17:c[0m[39mhmod +x $this_dir/dav1d_fuzzer_mt[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m18[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m19[0m[39m:$this_dir/dav1d_fuzzer_mt [0m[32m"$@"[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m20[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m22[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m23[0m[39m:# done, unset it[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;92m24:c[0m[39mhmod -x $this_dir/dav1d_fuzzer_mt[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Diagnose Root Cause[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The OSS-Fuzz runner mounts `[0m[35m/[0m[95mout[0m[39m` after running `meson install`; because [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mneither `dav1d_fuzzer` nor `dav1d_fuzzer_mt` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mnor the NO_OOM wrapper[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m have Meson [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minstall rules, no executable is placed into `[0m[35m/[0m[95mout[0m[39m` with proper mode.  As a result, [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[35m/out/[0m[95mdav1d_fuzzer_mt[0m[39m` either does not exist or exists without +x, yielding [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mâ€œPermission deniedâ€ and status [0m[1;36m126[0m[39m.[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Preserve Existing Logic[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - We must not touch harness/fuzzing scripts.  The wrapper script [0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`dav1d_fuzzer_mt@NO_OOM` and the C-code fuzzer logic remain unchanged.[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - We only augment Meson build definitions in `tests/libfuzzer/meson.build`, [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfollowing the pattern in `examples/meson.build` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mwhich uses `install : true` for [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`dav1dplay`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Patch Plan: Amend tests/libfuzzer/meson.build[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   a. For each fuzzer target [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`dav1d_fuzzer` and `dav1d_fuzzer_mt`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Add `install: true` so Meson will create an installed binary.[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Override the install directory to OSS-Fuzzâ€™s prefix [0m[1;39m([0m[39mi.e. `[0m[35m/[0m[95mout[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m so the [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexecutable lands at `[0m[35m/out/[0m[95mdav1d_fuzzer[0m[1;39m[[0m[39m_mt[0m[1;39m][0m[39m`.[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Ensure the install mode preserves executability [0m[1;39m([0m[39mdefault `[0m[1;36m0755[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   b. Install the NO_OOM wrapper script:[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Use Mesonâ€™s `configure_file` or `install_data` to copy [0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`dav1d_fuzzer_mt@NO_OOM` into the install prefix as `dav1d_fuzzer_mt`.[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Set `install_mode: [0m[32m'0755'[0m[39m` to guarantee it is executable.[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - This wrapper will sit at `[0m[35m/out/[0m[95mdav1d_fuzzer_mt[0m[39m` [0m[1;39m([0m[39moverwriting the raw [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbinary[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, matching the runnerâ€™s invocation.[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - The wrapper itself toggles exec bits on the real meson-installed binary [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39malso in `[0m[35m/[0m[95mout[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m when invoked, then toggles them off, exactly preserving its [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moriginal semantics.[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   c. Retain build-by-default and thread dependenciesâ€”only enrich the install [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mphase.[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Implementation Steps[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. Open `tests/libfuzzer/meson.build`.[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. Locate the `[0m[1;35mexecutable[0m[1;39m([0m[32m'dav1d_fuzzer'[0m[39m, [0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` and [0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mexecutable[0m[1;39m([0m[32m'dav1d_fuzzer_mt'[0m[39m, [0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` definitions.[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m. Add within each:[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        install : true,[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        install_dir : [0m[1;35mget_option[0m[1;39m([0m[32m'prefix'[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m,[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m. Immediately after those, add a `configure_file` stanza:[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        wrapper = [0m[1;35mconfigure_file[0m[1;39m([0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          input: [0m[32m'dav1d_fuzzer_mt@NO_OOM'[0m[39m,[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          output: [0m[32m'dav1d_fuzzer_mt'[0m[39m,[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          install: true,[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          install_dir: [0m[1;35mget_option[0m[1;39m([0m[32m'prefix'[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m,[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          install_mode: [0m[32m'0755'[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;36m5[0m[39m. Run `meson configure builddir --[0m[33mprefix[0m[39m=[0m[35m/[0m[95mout[0m[39m && ninja -C builddir install`.[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;36m6[0m[39m. Verify that `[0m[35m/out/[0m[95mdav1d_fuzzer_mt[0m[39m` is now the wrapper [0m[1;39m([0m[39mmode [0m[1;36m0755[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[35m/out/[0m[95mdav1d_fuzzer_mt.real[0m[39m` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mor the raw binary[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m exists and is toggled appropriately[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mby the wrapper.[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;36m7[0m[39m. Re-run the OSS-Fuzz Docker reproduction; expect no Permission Denied.[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Justification[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - By mirroring the `install : true` pattern from `examples/meson.build`, we [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mensure the fuzzer binaries are shipped to `[0m[35m/[0m[95mout[0m[39m` with correct permissions.[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Installing the NO_OOM wrapper as the entrypoint script at [0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[35m/out/[0m[95mdav1d_fuzzer_mt[0m[39m` preserves existing harness expectations, while the wrapperâ€™s[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mchmod dance ensures the raw binary is only briefly executable.[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No external or harness code is modified; all changes live in the projectâ€™s [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mMeson definitions. This isolates the change to the build/install logic and [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msatisfies OSS-Fuzzâ€™s requirement to leave harnesses intact.[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. Potential Side Effects and Mitigation[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - If the raw and wrapper names collide, ensure the real binary has a distinct [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfilename [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g. `.real` suffix[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m before installing the wrapper. Alternatively, [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minstall the real binary under its Meson name [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`dav1d_fuzzer_mt`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and install the [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwrapper under the same name via `configure_file`, which will override it on [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minstallâ€”this is acceptable because Fuzz runner only cares about the wrapperâ€™s [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbehavior.[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Verify no existing tests depend on the binaries being in [0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`build/tests/libfuzzer`â€”all tests should pass against wrapper logic in `[0m[35m/[0m[95mout[0m[39m`.[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This strategy aligns with other OSS-Fuzz projects and has minimal maintenance [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mburden.[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Root Cause Analysis[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The Meson build definitions for the two fuzz targets [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`dav1d_fuzzer` and [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`dav1d_fuzzer_mt`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m do not include an `install: true` directive. As a result, when [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mOSS-Fuzz invokes `ninja install` into `$OUT`, the fuzz binaries are neither [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minstalled nor have their execute bits preserved in `[0m[35m/[0m[95mout[0m[39m`. This causes the [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mâ€œPermission deniedâ€ error when the base-runner tries to invoke [0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[35m/out/[0m[95mdav1d_fuzzer_mt[0m[39m`.[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Patch Plan[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Edit the file `tests/libfuzzer/meson.build`.[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - In the `[0m[1;35mexecutable[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` stanza for both `dav1d_fuzzer` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m51[0m[39mâ€“[0m[1;36m60[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`dav1d_fuzzer_mt` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m61[0m[39mâ€“[0m[1;36m70[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, add the keyword argument:[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       install : true,[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     just before the closing parenthesis.[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No other changes are required. This ensures that:[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     â€¢ On `ninja install` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mwhich OSS-Fuzz runs with `--[0m[33mdestdir[0m[39m=$OUT`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, the [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexecutables are copied into the installation prefix under `$OUT`.  [0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     â€¢ Meson preserves the execute permission bit, so the binaries become runnable [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mas `[0m[35m/out/[0m[95mdav1d_fuzzer[0m[39m` and `[0m[35m/out/[0m[95mdav1d_fuzzer_mt[0m[39m`.[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Implementation Steps[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   a. Open `tests/libfuzzer/meson.build`.  [0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   b. Locate the block:[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```meson[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      dav1d_fuzzer = [0m[1;35mexecutable[0m[1;39m([0m[32m'dav1d_fuzzer'[0m[39m,[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         â€¦,[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         kwargs: fuzzer_link_lang[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      and change it to:[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```meson[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      dav1d_fuzzer = [0m[1;35mexecutable[0m[1;39m([0m[32m'dav1d_fuzzer'[0m[39m,[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         â€¦,[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   c. Likewise, locate:[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```meson[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      dav1d_fuzzer_mt = [0m[1;35mexecutable[0m[1;39m([0m[32m'dav1d_fuzzer_mt'[0m[39m,[0m                               [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```meson[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      dav1d_fuzzer_mt = [0m[1;35mexecutable[0m[1;39m([0m[32m'dav1d_fuzzer_mt'[0m[39m,[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         â€¦,[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   d. Save the file and commit the patch.  [0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   e. Trigger the OSS-Fuzz build. Confirm in the build logs that Mesonâ€™s `install` [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mstep copies both fuzzers into `[0m[35m/[0m[95mout[0m[39m` with `-rwxr-xr-x` permissions.[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Justification[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Following the existing pattern shown in `examples/meson.build` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mwhere [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`dav1dplay` is installed via `install: true`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, this change aligns the fuzz targets [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwith the rest of the projectâ€™s installable binaries.  [0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - It does not alter any harness code, runtime logic, or tests. Existing [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfunctionality and tests remain untouched.  [0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - It directly addresses the â€œPermission deniedâ€ symptom by ensuring the fuzzer [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbinaries are present and executable in `[0m[35m/[0m[95mout[0m[39m`, satisfying the base-runnerâ€™s [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexpectations.[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Side-Effects & Mitigation[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No semantic changes to the library or fuzz logic.  [0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The only side-effect is that the fuzz binaries become part of the install [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtreeâ€”this is desired for OSS-Fuzz integration.  [0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No other installable artifacts are modified.  [0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. Verification[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - After the patched build completes, run:[0m                                        [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     docker run â€¦ -v [0m[35m/path/to/build/out/[0m[95mdav1d[0m[39m:[0m[35m/[0m[95mout[0m[39m â€¦ base-runner reproduce [0m         [2m                [0m
